## Section 001: Local Vision Media Patterns
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed title names the theme without its operating claim, that reliable local vision analysis is mostly input preparation, resizing, filename sanitization, and staging, done before the model ever runs
- **supporting_reason:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the source opens by naming its three handled pitfalls, oversized images causing timeouts, Unicode filenames breaking paths, and batch processing, so the theme's identity is pitfall management around a fixed local model
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the guidance is hardware-coupled, its numbers assume a 24GB M4 mini running qwen3.5:4b on Ollama, and transfer to other hosts only as a pattern, not as figures
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: this reference operationalizes the local-vision-ollama skill's rules and does not evaluate alternative vision models
- **revision_decision:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to open with the input-preparation claim, name the four critical rules, and state the hardware and runtime the numbers assume
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the skill inverts where quality effort goes, none of its rules concern prompts or model choice at analysis time, all four police the file path between disk and model
### Question 02: What is the recommended default, and why?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 02 on recommended default: the defensible default is to pre-resize every image to 800px longest edge, sanitize names through Python listdir and join, stage in /tmp with clean ASCII names, and keep concurrency at two to three
- **supporting_reason:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 02 on recommended default: prefer that default because the source opens by naming its three handled pitfalls, oversized images causing timeouts, Unicode filenames breaking paths, and batch processing, so the theme's identity is pitfall management around a fixed local model
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 02 on recommended default: do not present the default as universal; the guidance is hardware-coupled, its numbers assume a 24GB M4 mini running qwen3.5:4b on Ollama, and transfer to other hosts only as a pattern, not as figures
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 02 on recommended default: the default assumes the following scope: this reference operationalizes the local-vision-ollama skill's rules and does not evaluate alternative vision models
- **revision_decision:** Section 001 "Local Vision Media Patterns", Question 02 on recommended default: make the default operational by stating both this action and its handoff: open with the input-preparation claim, name the four critical rules, and state the hardware and runtime the numbers assume

## Section 003: Pattern Scoreboard Ranking Table
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 003 "Pattern Scoreboard Ranking Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed scoreboard scores corpus hygiene while the skill's own load-bearing patterns go unranked, pre-resize first, sanitize filenames through Python, stage in /tmp, and bound concurrency
- **supporting_reason:** Section 003 "Pattern Scoreboard Ranking Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the source numbers its rules and marks resizing as rule one with an ALWAYS, so the ranking it implies is explicit and should be transmitted

## Section 008: Verification Gate Command Set
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed gate names the corpus verifier while the theme's real gates are operational, image dimensions checked after resize, staged paths confirmed, and a bounded test analysis before a batch
- **supporting_reason:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the skill's reliability comes from preparation steps, so verification means proving the preparation happened, dimensions, paths, and timing
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: dimension checks prove resize but not content integrity, a corrupted copy passes the size gate
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: the gate set defines what must pass before a batch analysis is trusted and does not implement the pipeline
- **revision_decision:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to add operational gates, sips or file inspection confirming 800px bounds, a staged-path check that all inputs live in /tmp with ASCII names, and a single-image smoke run timed under thirty seconds before batches
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 008 "Verification Gate Command Set", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the smoke run doubles as a routing gate, a single resized image that still runs slow implicates the .env model routing, catching the config pitfall before a batch amplifies it

- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 011 "Decision Tradeoff Guide", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: judging images small by eye fails, dimensions and file size need checking because Retina captures look ordinary

## Section 020: Failure Mode Table

## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed bullets classify verification failures generically and never carry this theme's retry rule, a timed-out image is retried smaller, not merely again
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the source's retry advice mutates the input, resize to 600px then retry, because repeating an unchanged oversized input deterministically reproduces the timeout
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: input-mutation retries apply to size failures, not to path errors, whose fix is re-staging rather than resizing
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: this governs both retrying pipeline calls and retrying reference-verification work, kept as two labeled layers
- **revision_decision:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to add the pipeline-layer rule, retries must change the failing condition, smaller image for timeouts, restaged path for name errors, fewer concurrent calls for OOM, with the config bump as the last resort
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that every legitimate retry in this skill is a downgrade of demand, smaller input, cleaner path, less concurrency, which makes retry-without-change detectable as a rule violation by diffing the two attempts

## Section 022: Observability Checklist
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed bullets recycle generic evidence records and never name this theme's evidence stream, the staging manifest, per-call timings, and the config snapshot in effect
- **supporting_reason:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the artifact section defines the manifest and the metrics section the timings, so observability means persisting both plus the routing config that determined which model ran
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: full manifest retention for every trivial call outgrows its value, the null-instance convention applies
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: this covers observing analysis sessions, not the Ollama server's own logs
- **revision_decision:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to recenter the checklist on session evidence, the manifest, call timings, error texts verbatim, and the AUXILIARY_VISION values in effect at run time
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 022 "Observability Checklist", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the config snapshot is the evidence most often missing when it matters, routing bugs are diagnosed by knowing which model actually served the call, which nothing else in the session records

## Section 024: Scale Boundary Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the pipeline is a single-host, single-model design, its concurrency ceiling and timeout budget define a throughput wall that no preparation discipline moves
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: scaling advice beyond one host is out of the source's scope and would be pure inference here
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: the boundaries bound this reference and its pipeline, not local vision as a technique
- **revision_decision:** Section 024 "Scale Boundary Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to add scale signals, batches outgrowing single-session review, sustained demand saturating the two-call ceiling, and non-raster or non-file inputs the staging rules cannot serve
